While the cosmic deception concept provides a framework, the story lacks a clear inciting incident or meaningful development. The brother subplot feels disconnected from the main narrative thread. The oscillating action is present physically but doesn't create narrative momentum. Despite these issues, the story maintains internal logic within its dreamlike framework.
